 a person like g d Agarwal can write
 wo likhte hai, '2014 ke lok-sabha chunaav tak to tum bhi swayan maa gangaji ke samajhadaar, laadle or maa ke prati samarpit betaa hone kii baat karte the par vah chunaav maa ke aashirwad or prabhu ram kii krupa se jitkar ab to tum maa ke hi kuch laalchee, vilasitapriy bete-betiyon ke samooh main funs gaye ho or un nalyakon kii vilasita ke saadhan jutaney ke liye jise tum log vikaas kehete ho, kabhi jal maarg ke naam se budhi maa ko bojha dhone vaala khachchar bana daalane chaahate ho, kabhi urja kii aavashyaktaa puri karne kiye hal kaa, gaadi kaa yaa kolhu jaisi mashiinon kaa bail
 ' ganga kitni saaf hui, yah baat ganga ko maaloom hogi

 sieji ne disambar 2017 main namaami gange ko lekar ek report di thi jisamen kaha tha, 'hamane 87 project ke sample kii jaanch kii thi

 in sabhi ke liye 7,992

 ye sieji ne kaha he

 do hazaar karod se adhik ke fund kaa istamaal nahin hua he
 This is a December 2017 report
 is saal agast main down tu arth ne ganga par ek report chhaapi thi jisamen saaf-saaf kaha tha march 2019 tak ganga ko saaf karne kaa lakshya he lekin ganga ko lekar pradhanmantri ke netritv main bani rashtriya ganga parishad kii ek bhi baithak nahin hui he
 This council was formed in October 2016 and the report of Down to Earth is dated 29 August 2018
 do saal main ek bhi baithak nahin hoti he
 Avikal Somvanshi reports that the National Ganga Council was formed to prevent and save pollution in the Ganges River
 iske gajet main he ki saal main ek baithak to hogi hi
 The National Ganga River Basin Authority (NGRBA) was formed in 2009 which was dissolved and the National Ganga Council was formed on 7 October 2016
 manmohan singh ke samay bani athurity kii paanch baithke hui thim
 Prime Minister Modi created a new council but not a single meeting was held in two years
 down tu arth kii report main he
 This was also the meeting of the NGRBA chaired by Uma Bharti in 2014 and 2015
 july 2016 main pradhanmantri modi kii adhyakshata main NGRBA kii ek baithak hui thi magar nai council bani to uske baad do saal tak baithak nahin hui
 Avikal Somvanshi has written that many calls were made to the Director General of National Mission for Clean Ganga but no response was received
 tippaniyan You will see that in your Hindi newspapers, there will be talk of sentiment about Ganga that Ganga is this, that is it, but you can hardly get the news related to Ganga in such a way that Down to Earth did

 4 dinon ke mahaparv chhath main aaj surya ko pehla arghya diya ja rahaa he
 Today, a crowd of Chhath Vratis thronged the ghats across the country to offer arghya to the setting sun
 patna se lekar mumbai tak shraddhalu vidhi-vidhaan se puja paath main jute hai

 chhath puri duniya kaa iklauta aisa parv jisamen ugte suraj ke saath duubate suraj kii bhi vandana kii jaati he, jal arpit kiya jaataa he
 The festival of Vandana of nature was celebrated only in the Purvanchal region of India, but during the time of confluence of the globalizing world and cultures, Chhath has become a Mahaparva
 chhath par raashi ke anusaar karen surya ko arpan, puri hogi har manokamnapatna se lekar dilli or mumbai tak nadi ghaaton par shraddhaluon kii bheed umad padi he
 In this mahaparva of four days, Chhath Vrati fast for 36 hours
 parv ke dauraan man or sharir kii shuddhta kii badi ahmiyat he
 It is believed that the sixth maiya has special kindness on children
 
 
 isliye santan kii salaamati kaa aashirwad paane ke liye bhi is vrath kii badi ahmiyat he

 ) Smartphone memory reduced? Don't want to delete photos and videos too? No problem
 aapke paas ab bhi bina external memory card lagaae memory badhaane kaa opshan he
 If you use whatsapp, it is possible that you would not have cleared its memory before this
 watsap kii memory clear karke aap apane smartphone kaa kaaphi spes bachaa sakate hai
 You will be surprised to see how much memory whatsapp consumes on your smartphone
 haalanki yah har yugers ke liye ek jaisaa nahin he
 Because some people use whatsapp less, some use much more
 aaie aapako bataate hai ki watsap kii memory clear karke apane smartphone kii storage ko kaise impruva kar sakate hai
 For this, you will have to click unnecessary chats
 storage yuses dekhne ke liye ye steps hanvotsapaki settings main jaaen
 Here you will see data and storage usage
 ise tap karen
 Here you will see the storage usage option in the list, tap it
 ab aapke saamne ek list dikhegi
 At the top here will be the chat which is consuming the most memory
 ise clic karke aap sari jaankaree dekh sakate hai
 How many photos are there, how much text is there, and all the spaces of the categories will be visible
 yahaan sabase neeche aapako manage kaa opshan dikhegaa
 You will get the option of Clear as soon as you tap it
 yahaan select karke aap puure chat ko hataa sakate hai
 Or you can remove photos, videos if you want
 agar aap chats or files delit nahin karnaa chaahate to
 
 aap files ko computer main seve bhaphi kar sakate hai
 For this, the mobile phone has to be connected to the computer
 apane smartphone kii settings me ja kar develaper opshan aneble karen or yahaan USB debugging par tap karen
 Now open the storage of mobile phone in your computer
 yahaan aapako whatsapp naam kaa foulder dikhegaa
 The folder will contain a media file
 ise copy karke apane computer main seve kar len
 Now by opening it, you can recover whatsapp images, whatsapp audio, whatsapp documents and whatsapp videos
 ab aapke paas do opshan hai
 If chats are not necessary for you, then delete everything directly
 agar aapke liye chats mahatvapurn hai to aap in kaa byaap le kar phir wo step pholo karen jo hamane aapako bataaya he
 By doing this, you can save a good amount of storage of your mobile

 The history of the seat: Madurai Lok Sabha seat was occupied by the Congress 7 times at most
 1952 main hue pehle loksabhaa chunaav main yahaan congress ne jeet darj kii thi
 But the Congress could not retain the seat for a long time and in the 1957 election the CPI snatched this seat

 Delhi High Court has started helpline number 1888 from today
 ye helpline desh kii pehali helpline hogi jo kisi court main shuru kii ja rahi he
 This help line will work in the working hours of the High Court
 dilli hai court desh kaa pehla hai court he jahaan ye suvidha di ja rahi he
 Earlier there was no help line facility in any court
 ye helpline aaj 4:30 baje se shuru ho chuki he
 Acting Chief Justice of Delhi High Court Geeta Mittal has started this help line
 is helpline kaa makasad court aane vaale pakshakaron, vakeelon or aam logon kii jaagarukta or madad ke liye he
 The purpose of starting this helpline of the High Court is also that those people who want to file a case but cannot advocate, can also be given legal information about what legal options they have
 iske alaava is helpline par phone karke koi bhi apane cese se judi jaankaree hasil kar saktaa he

 is help line par sabhi disabled bhi kol kar sakate hai
